		$(this).css('background-color','#ededed');

    var didScroll;
    var lastScrollTop = 0;
    var delta = 160;
    var navbarHeight = $('#header-inner-pages','#footer-buttons-floating').outerHeight();
    $(window).scroll(function(event){
        didScroll = true;
    });
    setInterval(function() {
        if (didScroll) {
            hasScrolled();
            didScroll = false;
        }
    }, 100);
    function hasScrolled() {
        var st = $(this).scrollTop();
        if (st > lastScrollTop && st > navbarHeight){
            $('#header-inner-pages').removeClass('nav-down').addClass('nav-up');
            $('#footer-buttons-floating').removeClass('nav-up').addClass('nav-down');
        } else {
            if(st === 0 || st <= 120) {
                $('#header-inner-pages').removeClass('nav-up').addClass('nav-down');
                $('#footer-buttons-floating').removeClass('nav-down').addClass('nav-up');
            }
        }
        lastScrollTop = st;
    } </script> </div> <div id="rankings" class="ng-scope"> <div class="container ng-scope" ng-controller="FooterCtrl as footer"> <h1 class="big-title text-center">Rankings</h1> <h2       closeMenu();
    })
    $('li[data-target="#MoreOptions"]').click(function () {
      $("#MyAccount").collapse('hide');
      defaultIcon('li[data-target="#MyAccount"]');
      changeIcon('li[data-target="#MoreOptions"]');
    });
    $('li[data-target="#MyAccount"]').click(function () {
      $("#MoreOptions").collapse('hide');
      defaultIcon('li[data-target="#MoreOptions"]');
      changeIcon('li[data-target="#MyAccount"]');
    });
    function defaultIcon(target) {
      $(target).collapse('hide');
      var el = $(target)[0];
      $(el).find('.icon').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-right');
    }
    function changeIcon(el) {
      var element = $(el)[0];
      if($(el)[0].classList.contains('collapsed')) {
        $(element).find('.icon').removeClass('fa-angle-right').addClass('fa-angle-down');
      } else {
        $(element).find('.icon').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-right');
      }
    }
    function closeMenu() {
      $('#menu-mobile-modal').modal('hide');
      $('#MyAccount').collapse('hide');
      $('#MoreOptions').collapse('hide');
      defaultIcon('li[data-target="#MyAccount"]');
      defaultIcon('li[data-target="#MoreOptions"]');
      // show search bar
      $('.scroll-control-cover').removeClass('hide-search').addClass('visible-search');
    }
    // function very old created in old version menu
    $("#menu-mobile-modal").on("show.bs.modal", function() {
      changeIconComplain();
      var top = $("body").scrollTop();
      $("body").css({
        'position': 'fixed',
        'overflow': 'hidden',
        'top': '0',
        'width': '100%',
        'height': '720px'
      });
    }).on("hide.bs.modal", function() {
        var top = $("body").position().top;
        $("body").css({
          'position': 'relative',
          'overflow': 'auto',
          'top': 0
        }).scrollTop(-top);
    });
    function changeIconComplain() {
      if(location.pathname === '/minha-conta/minhas-reclamacoes/') {
        $('.complain-gray').css('display','none');
        $('.complain-blue').css('display','initial');
        $('#complain-item').addClass('active');
      } else {
        $('.complain-gray').css('display','initial');
        $('.complain-blue').css('display','none');
        $('#complain-item').removeClass('active');
      }
    }
    // Fix bug scroll in mobile
    $('#menu-mobile-modal').on('click touchstart', function() {
      if($('#menu-mobile-modal').scrollTop() === 0) {
        $('#menu-mobile-modal').scrollTop($('#menu-mobile-modal').scrollTop() + 1);
      } else {
        $('#menu-mobile-modal').scrollTop($('#menu-mobile-modal').scrollTop() - 1);
      }
    })
    $('.changeEmail').click(function() {
      setTimeout(function (){
        $('#modal-user-mail').modal('show');
      },1000);      
    }); </script></div> <!-- ngInclude: 'views/partials/footer.html' --><div ng-include="'views/partials/footer.html'" class="ng-scope"><div style="clear:both" class="ng-scope"></div> <!-- ngIf:
